 vah aamjivan ke kathankon ke saath hi manch ke lekhak bhi the

 yah jaananaa kam mjedaar nahin ki kamtanath ne ek sarkari karmchaaree, ek lekhak or ek actor kii tarah apni alag-alag chhap chodi

 pehle main aisi kahaniyaan hai, jinamein maanviya sambandh or paariwarik rishte pramukhataa se dikhte hai

 He came into legend at a time when 'new story', 'katha movement', 'village-life' and 'conscious' story were replaced by characters belonging to the middle class of the city, town, for whom jealousy, Tales of sex, frustration, panic, loneliness, revenge, strangeness and success were everything
 kamtanath in prabhaavon se dur rahe
 He touched this same class, but in his own way

 a play based on the stories of Guy the Mopansa, written as 'women'

 The 86 km long road connecting Chisumale and Demachak villages is of strategic importance
 ye gaanv purvi kshetra main bharat-china seemaa se mahaj kuch hi duuri par sthit hai
 Praising the BRO personnel for taking up this difficult task, the project's Chief Engineer Brigadier DM Purveemath said that the road to such a high altitude was full of challenges
 unhone kaha ki is jagah kii jalwaayu nirmaan gatividhiyon ke liye hameshaa hi mushkil rahati he
